There are several ways to perform the cautery, either three or four, by arranging them according to the length of the mouse, as I described in the treatment of the liver; and do not rush your hand over the entire cautery, and let the patient lie on his back; there is another way to perform the cautery that involves heating the cauter that has two nerves, as we showed in the dislocation of the shoulder; lift the tissue that is near the mouse, or the side where the patient's pain comes from, and elevate the swellings you lift the tissue according to the length of the body, and the cautery should be according to the width of the body.
Aprés i boute les II ners enflamez tant que li keurs soit perciez de l’autre part, et puis trai fuers le cautere, et ensi en i avra IIII Et se tu vues, si cauterize a tot le cautere a III ners.	 After putting the two nerves inflamed in such a way that the other part is pierced, pull the fire cautery out, and thus there will be four openings; if you see, cauterize the entire cautery on three nerves.
Aprés le cure quant il a geteit porriture par lonc tens, et ce vaut mues que li autre des cures devant dites.	 After the treatment when pus has come out for a long time, it is necessary to use the other treatments mentioned before.
de ydropisie	And from the dropsy
Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».	 Cautery does not work on dropsy, except in the manner called "asclytes".
Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis; et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur.	 When the cure is done according to the methods that we have said in divisions, and the treatment does not help at all, then it is necessary to make four cauteries around the abdomen, one above the stomach, one above the liver, one above the spleen, two behind the back near the spine, and one at the place of pain; and let the cauterizations be close to the thickness of the skin.
Aprés laisse le cautere aovert por giter porriture lonc tens, et ne lassier mie la cure dou malaide aprés le cautere; et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les .ij. ententions avec l’aide de Deu.	After leaving the cautery open for a long time to drain pus, do not cease treating the patient after the cautery; and healing will hasten, and the two intentions (presumably referring to life and health) will be together with the help of God.
Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit; et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.	The shape of the fire cautery for the belly is like the cleaver that we have shown before; and for the back, it should be olive-shaped, as has been described earlier.
de l’enfleure des piez	the swelling of the feet
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire; et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	 When the feet are swollen in a patient who is edematous (dropical), and filled with yellow fluid, you must cauterize on the back of the foot between the little finger and the ring finger; and dip your hand with the cautery without turning it.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	 And do not enter too deeply, so as not to burn the yellow fluid excessively; and let the cautery be in this shape:
Aprés fai sus .ij. jambes .ij. cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire; et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe; et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse; aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	Afterwards do two cauteries on both legs at the tip of the scalpel; and let the cauteries be long, one beneath the knee in front and the other outside the leg; and keep the cauterized areas open for a long time to heal, as is necessary; then treat the other wounds as we have said.
de la menoison	In the treatment of the dislocated shoulder:
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures; et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai .i. grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule; et .iiij. cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout .i. cautere clavile subtil, et .ij. cauteres sus les hainches.	When the swelling of the belly comes from coldness and moisture, as the digestive and retentive properties which are in the stomach and intestines are disturbed and cannot be cured by methods of healing; and you see the patient suffering greatly and with strong symptoms, then do one large cautery on the stomach according to what was said before or fire cauterization of the stomach, around the belly four subtle cauteries, and one small subtle cautery near the navel and two subtle cauteries on the hips.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et .i. cautere sus chaicun yle, et .ij. petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	And if you see abundant moisture and the patient suffering, make a cautery on the shoulder, and one cautery on each joint, and two small cauterizations on the stomach beneath it, for the cure is beneficial when there is good aid.
de la cure des emorroydes	Of the treatment of hemorrhoids
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres: III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois; et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile; et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	 When hemorrhoids are based or one or more, and are old and filled with thick cold and moist corrupted fluids, and have been treated as we have said in the divisions, it is of no use to do cauteries: III on the spine of the back, that which is completely deflected under the loinbone and triangular, and the cautery below the buttock; and if you think that his stomach is chilled and meat not cooked, and the face swells, then the face receives a large cautery on the stomach as previously said, and another on the liver, and another on the spleen with the entire cautery nail; and leave the cautery open for a long time.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	 After healing the shoulder when it is healed.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	of the carnivorous disease called "thelul"
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble .i. raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit; et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort; fai ceu une fois ou .ij., et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit; aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez; et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	When you treat althelul, if the cautery appears to be similar to a razor, then heat it and apply it all around the althelul wound; leave your hand there so that the cautery comes to the opening of the vein, thus cutting off the blood flow. Do this once or twice, and if there is much althelul, cauterize each spot as we have said; after applying ointments, allow it to heal until it is healed; if you cauterize a large cautery on the skin, it will provide more aid.
de plaie mal curee	From badly healed wound
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When the patient cannot bear incision or opening, we will speak about it in its place; this disease can only be cured by cautery.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	 If a fistula comes, and it is swollen and filled with pus and decayed matter, you should test the whole tent in every way, and be sure that you know the entire tent how much it heals.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing; et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	 After heating the cautery that resembles a razor, insert it into the fistula according to the size of the tent that has entered, and repeat the cauterization as much as the body requires to burn and decay; once, or II or III, depending on the amount of pus needed; and beware not to burn the nerve that is nearby, and the large veins.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans; aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement; et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font; et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	 If the fistula goes to the body of the bladder and intestine, beware of these places, and do not perform this action outside of a charnu (a surgical instrument), and believe that it is not dangerous; after healing the shoulder when it is healed, if the shoulder is sutured and the matter has been removed for a long time, then know that the shoulder is healed completely; and if the matter is not removed, know that the bone is broken, and corrupt the bone in its place; and thus as one of those whom we will say in his place.
de la maladie des reins	Of the disease of the kidneys
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit; et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra .iij. cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	When pain in the loins comes from cold and bloating, and it does not take on female form, then you must apply fire cautery to the kidneys from both sides with the small-headed iron we have mentioned earlier; and if we cauterize it in the middle, it will have 4 cauteries in a line, and they will be more effective.
de la vessie	Of the bladder
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et .i. a destre et .i. a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce; et li fais .i. cautere defuers le dos, ou .ij. se tu en as besoing; et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	When the bladder is weakened by cold and moisture, causing the patient to retain urine, then apply fire cautery on the part of the bladder located behind it, where the pubic hair begins, one on each side, and each cautery should be as long as your thumb; also make a cautery at the back, if needed; and use the small-headed iron in the shape described earlier.
de la marris	of the marriage
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde; et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor: adonques covient il c’on li faice .iij. cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et .ij. cauteres defuers le dos; et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	When the marriage is cold and moist and does not allow conception, and the flowers are corrupted and their term is delayed; and when they come, it causes great pain: then it is necessary to apply four cauterizations around the womb, as we have said regarding the bladder cautery, and two cauterizations behind the back; and let the cauterization be incision-like, as we have said.
de la hainche	of the itch
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble; et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a .i. cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle; et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	When the humors viscous descend towards the pit of the itch, and for this reason it moves away from its place, and the signs are that the thigh is longer than the other when measured together; and the place of the departure is found if it is necessary to cauterize the patient on the pit of the itch with one cautery resembling a circle, and sign in front of the place around the pit as it turns, so that the pit is within the circle; and let the cauterization be such as when the stomach has been cauterized.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai .iij. cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs; et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if this fire cautery is not present, make four large olive oil cauterizations instead, and let them be as deep as all the others; and let it heal when it is healthy.
de la dolor de la hainche	of the pain from the hernia
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene: adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	When pain comes in the area of the hernia and it is caused by coldness and moisture, and the patient is cured as we have said in the division, but the cure is not effective, and the disease is old; then you must purge the patient of the gross humors with fetid pills or other good-seeming pills.
Aprés li fai cautere; et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres: c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	 After that, do fire cautery; and the method of fire cautery is according to two ways: namely, with burning substances, and cauterization by fire.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz: que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire; aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	 Fire cauterization can be done in several ways, one of which is to cauterize on the belly of the hernia in three triangular cauteries according to this form, making a good and deep incision and leaving space between each cautery the size of a thumb, and let the cauteries be olive-shaped. Sometimes a cauterization is made in the middle on the head of the hernia, for which there are four according to this form:
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche; mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if you wish, cauterize at the circular cautery that we have previously mentioned in the dislocation of the hernia; but do it in such a way that the circles enclose the entire hernia, and all the edges should be burned.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	 And this is the method for treating sciatica when the pain remains in the loin and does not reach as far as the thigh nor the leg.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc; et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur; et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	 If the pain reaches as far as the thigh and the leg, you should perform cautery where the patient indicates that the pain is located, and the cautery shall be made four fingers above the ankle on the left side, a little bit; it can be a surgical cautery, but the thickness of the coal used must be thin; and if the patient feels that the pain extends up to two fingers or near there, you should cauterize where they feel the pain with three fingers or four on the cautery which is called "poins".
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus; et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	And if necessary, do more; and if the pain is below the knee towards the thigh, make a fire cautery with a knife or circular cautery, but be careful in all your cauteries not to let the cautery burn the nerves and large arteries, and not to cause greater damage and contraction to the patient.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	 And I myself have seen many who made fire cautery on the heel of the foot, and they let it grow so much that the leg was swollen all over, and the toes as well, and all the toes were pierced and corrupted.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	 After a belly solution where he died.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	 And if the pain is in two places at once, do cautery on one and the other, according to this method.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce; et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait; et c’est li forme:	 And the wise men said in the cautery of the ankle, as follows: make the iron like a small nail or slightly less, and it should be between the ankles or one between the ankles to a distance equal to the size of a nut; and the anvils should be above each part, and they should be shaped like nuts, and have a well-made anvil; this is its form:
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit; et lou cauterize une fois .i. cautere reont et lou laisse .iij. jors; et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens; aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	And heat it until it turns completely red and boils, then place it on top of the sick person's wound and turn it towards the healthy side; and cauterize once with a firebrand. Let it rest for four days, then apply a plaster made of butter, keep the wound open for a long time; after treating with ointment until it heals.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent; et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	Albuhasim says that we should use this cautery sparingly due to the fear of its appearance and those who rarely use it; however, it is one of the good cauterizations, which can be endured, and there where it cauterizes.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi; et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	 The fire cautery of medicine is such that you make the instrument inside hinges in this way, cutting along the edge of the door, and it should be made of iron or steel with a long handle, and on top it should have two prongs, and between each prong the thickness of a finger; and they should be open and above, and join together according to this form:
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche; aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	 After placing the hinge-board on the sick person lying on his side, put your hand almost above the hinge-board; after that, throw in between the two circles of hot iron that has been heated by the fire pot for an hour, and let the patient endure the heat and burning from it.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu; et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit; et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait; et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	 For it burns like biting into flesh, and when the bites have passed, take your hand with the instrument and gently lift the wound edge, and leave it thus for three days, and cover it with butter until the blackish scab is removed; and leave it for three days so that pus can drain out; and this would be the last help after the ointment treatment until it heals.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument; et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	 If the pain has spread to the thigh or leg, do as you have done in the wound edge: that is how hot water is used, and I have written or explained its method of treatment for medical correction.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	 Take alkali and hot live coal, equal amounts of each, grind them together, and put them in a new pot.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir; et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main; et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	 Have a small hole covered so that the tip of a razor can enter; and pour this pot onto another well-sealed pot, then put alkali and coal and water on top, until there are two layers of powder that you have well stirred with your hand; and leave it like that until the water and steam and smoke or pot evaporate, then take all of that ash, and pour it over the coal and the alkali as before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	 And when it is hot, it is administered for various medical tasks and other cauteries of different members because it does the same work as fire, and if with other medicines that are used to cauterize a wound such as thistle and honey, coal with soap, all these things mixed together.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	 And Galen tells us of a cure in which a nobleman was healed from the pain of the hernia and sciatica, and he praised it much, and said that no other treatment was used, and that he became healthy once when this cure was performed, and he bathed himself as he instructs hereafter.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie; et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	 And he says to take green litharge in powdered and dry form, grind it well with a little fat, place it on the hernia and the thigh and leg where the pain is felt, and press it; and leave it for 3 hours until the patient no longer feels the burning sensation.
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	 And then make him enter the bath until his body is slightly warmed, and make him lie down, and the pain will leave completely and he will be cured.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	 And know that no one should use fire cautery of such medications unless after the evacuation of the body.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout; et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	 And Dioscorides says that when the sciatic vein is cauterized with goat's fat, it helps much; and the cautery should be done in this manner.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	 Take linen and beat it with old oil, and place it over the furrow which is between the big toe of the foot and the other one which is called the "fossicle".
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains; et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee; et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	 Afterwards take dried goat's fat and heat it until it becomes charcoal, place it on the linen and leave it until it has been absorbed; then repeat this process again, and do not stop repeating until you believe with your senses that it reaches the bone, and that the pain stops; and this method of cautery is called "cautery of goat's fat".
de la dolor dou dos	of the pain in the back
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back, either by falling or from impact or excessive evacuation, or from similar causes of cold matter spreading, none of these cases are worth cauterization, unless it is due to the influx of cold matter.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne .v. cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir; et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»; et se tu vues, fai .iij. cauteres ou .iiij. au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	It is necessary afterwards that the patient be bled with pills or other similar things on the back where the pain is, three marked lines deep, and in each line 5 or more cauteries according to their power and quantity that the patient can bear; and the cautery should be made as the one called "poins"; and if you see, make 4 cauteries or 2 at a medium-sized cautery according to this form:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor; et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	This disease often comes to small children, and the signs of its onset are that they have a tightened throat when they are lying down, and fear; you will find it in the lower spine at the back and in the appearance that comes upon other spines.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this thing and intend to cure it, cauterize it with the fire cautery according to this form.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	 The fire cautery increases every part of the spine.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	 And if you see, cauterize around the spine with the cautery pointing to two or three lines, and let the tips be close to each other.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	 After curing the joint until it is healed as we have said, make sure you do not administer the cautery in the hollow of a nerve.
de la dolor des jointes	of the pain of the joints
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere: fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	When pain in joints is due to moisture that affects every member of the body, and when pain comes in feet, which are called "gout" properly, and when it is caused by coldness and medicines cannot cure it, it is cured by cauteries in this manner: make the patient sit with their leg bent at the joint, and the cautery should be olive-shaped according to this form.
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	 And if it is necessary to prick on the pelvis, make the cauterization with the whole cautery, as they claim "point".
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire; et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	 And if the pains come up to the knees and other joints, which happens often, make cauterization on each knee with three or four cauteries on each side, using an olive-shaped cautery; and if you need more, do more, but do not hold your hand too far away that the thickness of the coal is burned.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	 And if the pains descend to the knees and the back, administer the fire cautery as we have said in its chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes; et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main; et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	 And if the pains are at the hands, make incisions around the wrists for two lines; and if there is no pain in the fingers, make incisions on each joint and on the hair of the hand; and if the pains come to the elbows or shoulders, cauterize each part, and be mindful of the patient and think about remedies.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	 For if you take good care of him and cleanse him with purgation, he will be healed with God's help.
de la routure dou syfac	From the cutting of the siphac
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor; et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre; aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors; puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	When rupture comes in hernias, and the testicles descend into the inguinal canal and this is new, if you wish to treat it, it must not be masturbated on that day; and it should use things which loosen the belly, so that the hernia descends from the belly; afterwards, make him sit on his back between your hands, and command him to hold his flank until the testicles are repositioned, and you pull them towards you, and sign of the healing under the rupture on the bone of the thumb, and at every sign that is similar to half a circle above the body; then heat the cautery in the shape described here:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	 until it becomes white and exudes blood.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu; et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier; et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains; puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os; et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere; que tu ne le brulasses; et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	 Then pull the muscles back to their place; and let the attendant hold his hand so it does not return; and work well on the thighs of the patient, put the cussin and the serjeant on the thighs, and the other on the affected area which holds the hands; then place the cautery on the sign all over your hand, and keep it straight and hold it until you reach the bone, and if you do not touch the bone the first time, try again until you reach the bone; be careful that the muscles do not jump when you perform the cautery, so as not to burn them; and so that the patient does not die or suffer harm.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	 And know that if you do not reach the bone during the cautery, your efforts are worth nothing.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure; aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee; aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee; et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	 And the cauteries for children should be subtle according to their size, and the same for adults according to theirs; after three days, cure the wound from the cautery with butter until the burn is removed; after that, use other remedies until it is healed, and let the patient lie on his back for forty days while the wound is healing well; and it is necessary that his exudations (discharge) be left unattended so that boils do not appear when he gets up to go to rooms.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors; et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire; et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	 After forty days, when he wants to get up, let him be given a good poultice and put it on for another forty days; keep him in bed with good rest, but do not let him work too much or drink and eat too much, nor let him cough too much; if he follows this instruction, he will be completely healed.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	 And I shall say after the treatment of amputation in its chapter.
de la routure dou ventre	of the rupture of the abdomen (lit: of the bursting of the belly)
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur; aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit; et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	 When roundworms come in other wombs and are recognized, and you see that they no longer grow, you should perform the amputation cautery according to its size, and it should be burned one-third of the thickness; afterwards, you should heal according to what has been said; and none of the ancients have said that it should be cauterized with a three-angled cautery according to this form:
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	 but first mark the location and make a line above the roundworm, and another below, and then place your hand on the entire sharp-pointed cautery.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	 But the first cauteries are lighter and more mobile.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	of old pain in any member
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	 When pain comes in any member, either from falling or being injured, and that pain lasts a long time, and medicine does not heal it, then you should cauterize with the cautery called "poins," and the cauterizing should be according to the length of the limb, its smallness, weakness, its virtue, its location for twisting, and its pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien; se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	 If it is healed by the first cautery, that is good; if not, start another cautery on top of the first one because it is customary for the cautery to move towards the limb that is closest, so you should perform the cauterizing as long as the patient remains unhealed.
de meselerie	When the humors are out of balance due to moisture and heat, and one feels pain or discomfort, it must be purged through purgation. This involves taking a mixture of wormwood, myrtle leaves, and bread soaked in vinegar, which will help to cleanse and cool the body. After this, you should drink a cold water concoction made from crushed ivy, plantain seeds, or other suitable herbs, which will further aid in balancing the humors and alleviating the discomfort.
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	 The cautery is sometimes helpful to a great extent, and equally so the patient who comes from the putrefaction of phlegm and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief: I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous; et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel; et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir; et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	 Can you see the patient to perform a fire cautery, ensure that the patient is not in the beginning stages and has been treated as we have described in the division, and does not bleed nor remain; if you fear that corruption will affect the entire patient, then perform V cauterizations on the head: take hold of the head with one hand, and the other toward the front to the end of the hair; and over both temples, and behind the occipital bone; leave your hand in place until the cautery reaches the bone, and so that the scorch marks come out from it so that the vapors of the gross humors can escape; then cauterize on the swelling according to what is before.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse; et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et .i. cautere en som lou neis, et .ij. cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et .vj. cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et .i. grant sus la crupie et .i. autre delez, et .ij. sus les .ij. espaules; et .ij. sus les coutes, et .ij. sus les tendrons dou pis, et .i. sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains; et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler; et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et .i. autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et .i. autre sus lou foie.	And if the disease is scattered everywhere, it clearly spreads; therefore, you must cauterize with the cauteries we have mentioned at each point: one cautery in the navel, and two on the spine of the neck, and six on the spine of the back, and one large one on the hip and one smaller one, and two on each shoulder; and two on the sides, and two on the tendons of the feet, and one on each joint of the hands and feet, and on the hollows of the hands; beware of nerves that are near the last calcaneum, do not burn them; and sometimes a cautery is made on the bone of the wrist, and one other on the bone of the stomach, and one other on the liver.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite; et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	 And know that the more you do with fire cautery, the more help it provides and benefits them; and know that the sick do not feel pain from cautery as the healthy do, because the body is already completely corrupt.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	 And it should be great and small according to the members and the joints, as you will find in the ways of iron smithing.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	 After curing the shoulder with flour several times with honey and other remedies until it is healed.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre; et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur; puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	 When a swelling appears in any limb and is cured by medicines, oils, plasters, but it is not healed, then do cautery on the limb according to its size and smallness; and let the cautery be slightly entering into the thick part of the skin; then cure with oil until it is healed.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure; et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	 And sometimes they make a fire cautery on the hand, foot, and back, at the exit of the nerve that makes the limb motionless, and thus if it is excised the vein; nevertheless no one should interfere with it unless he is knowledgeable about the members and the exits of moving nerves of the body.
de albaras	Of ulcers or sores
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color; puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie; et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	When the disease called "albaras" is developed, and the medicine engine has no effect on it, then cauterize with a cautery of about half an inch deep according to the thickness of the skin, until the blister is removed and its color changes; then cure with flour and lentils mixed with rose oil and plantain leaves, and blood from a horse and crane, each one part; and mix everything together, and bind it with a cloth, and apply it to the place until it heals.
li cure de chancre par cautere	Cure syphilis by cauterization
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	 When a boil begins and you wish to stop it, if you cauterize, do so with the circular fire cautery all around the circumference of the boil.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre; et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois; et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	 Nevertheless the wise say that one should cauterize also in the middle of the boil; but it does not seem good to me because I fear that it will be ulcerated and corrupted, and I have seen it happen once before; a more appropriate thing is that it should be cauterized around, with the fire cautery which is called "circular", as we have said in the discussion on fire cauteries.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	Of the swelling which cannot grow
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens; et tu la vues haster de meurer: adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant; aprés le laisse ensi.	 When someone has a disease called "adubelati", which is slow to heal or because of the excess it causes, or because of the patient's age when he becomes decrepit (meaning very old) and has little blood, or because of the time; and you see it hastening to heal: then cauterize it with many small cauteries, pricking around it; after that, leave it as it is.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	 Then it will hasten to heal.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you see that the wound is pierced completely with all the cautery, heat the cautery in this manner:
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	 And put your hand in the middle of that disease called "adubelati" as long as the cauteries have pierced through, and let the cauteries be such that the patient feels no pain from them in this manner so that the course of the pustule is clear.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	 After the patient has recovered completely.
li cure dou feu par fer	the fire cure with iron
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	 Another kind of disease called "corroding", and it is nothing but an eating away of a limb because it consumes them as fire consumes dry wood.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est; aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	 If you see this disease in a place that can be burned with cautery along with fire, then gently heat the cauteries, both small and large, according to where the disease is; after burning all parts until you reach all the corruption and there remains nothing of it, everything corrupted should be removed.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	 And then leave it for three days and put on the affected areas softened cauteries made with oil until the burns caused by fire are removed, and all the corruption.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	 After the cure of ointments generating heat.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin; et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	 And if you see after three days that healthy char does not come out, it is good; and if not, repeat the fire cautery on the corrupt part of the body.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu; mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division: pren la quant tu en as mestier.	 And this purging is sometimes cured with medicinal bleeding instead of fire cautery; but nevertheless fire cautery is more helpful, and I have already said the treatment of medicinal bleeding in its division: take it when needed.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	The growing hairs should be allowed to remain long and equal on the feet;
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	 Often happens that in the foot through an opening comes a disease called "close" according to our intention, and it is a large thing swollen which breaks the foot.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	 And the cauteries of this disease are according to two ways.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	 This is to know fire cautery, and hot water cautery.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges; aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou; et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture; puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	 To know fire cautery, heat the iron to a point like a pen of hot coal, made from good iron that can pierce through all sides, and have fine edges; then place it on the nail and rotate your hand around the nail until it reaches the head of the nail; leave it there for three days until it begins to pus; then make a plaster with coarsely ground herbs and oil, and leave the plaster on top of everything all night, and the nails will shrink and be removed from their roots.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then heal the wound with healing salve until it is healed.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude; et est en teil maniere: pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues; et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine; et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre; puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	 And if it [the shoulder] has been dislocated by going out through the body, and this happens frequently in hands and feet, you should bring forth hot cautery; and it is to be done in this manner: take a cane made of iron or bone, or a pen from a plowshare, and place it on the nail and the tendon [or ligament], which means to burn warts; and place the cane so that it surrounds all around, then put a little hot tar there and hold your hand well, and press your hand as you turn so that the edge of the cane comes to the root of the nail, and may find the hot tar penetrating deep down to the root; and let the patient endure for an hour a little bit of the burning of the hot tar; then leave it like this, and it will all fall out with all its roots.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	 As another does afterwards, while you cauterize all those on the body, then treat with ointments that soothe pain.
li cure dou trembler	The cure for trembling
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices .iiij. cauteres ou .iv. sus l’espinee dou dos, .i. cautere entre chescune espinee; et .i. cautere ou pez, et .i. sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire; si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	For someone who is trembling due to cold or quarter fever or something else, you should perform four or five cauterizations on the spine of the back, one between each vertebra; and one in the buttock, and one on the stomach with an olive-oil cautery; this will stop the trembling and hasten recovery from the illness.
des pustules puans	pus-filled boils
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	 Sometimes, from the body's outside appear baths of pus or boils that come from large, corrupted matter.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule: un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	 Firstly, when they appear, it is necessary to make a fire-cauterization on each head of the boil: a subtle cautery of mirte stick or one made from the long root of aristoloche, or the cauterizer made from lentil seeds.
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez; mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	 And sometimes they are cauterized at the beginning when they appear in this way and they cannot grow further, but the excess is broken down from which they come, and they heal; however, it must be done after the evacuation of blood.
quant li artere est copee	when an artery is cut
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses; et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	Often, there is great bleeding from the cut artery that comes out at the wound or incision of an abscess, or during cauterization of a member, and similar things; it is a very serious matter to bleed excessively.
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus; puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge; puis empren .i., ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	And whenever this happens to anyone, quickly place your thumb on the wound of the vein, and hold it very tightly until the blood is calmed beneath your thumb, and no more gout exits; then take olive oil cauteries, both small and large until they are all red; then take .i., either large or small depending on the wound and the location where the arteries flow, and place the cautery on that vein where you hold your thumb, and hold the cautery in that position until the blood is coagulated.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement .i. autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	And if it jumps fiercely when you hold your thumb on the vein, and the cautery is extinguished, take hastily another one of the cauteries that are by the fire.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez; et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide; et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des .iiij. manieres que nos avons dit: ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc; et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	And do not stop doing this one after the other until the blood is coagulated; and be careful not to burn the nerve that is exposed, and let no other harm come to the patient; and know that when blood flows from an artery, it cannot be coagulated well if the artery is large, unless this is done by one of the four methods that we have mentioned: either by cautery, or by extraction when it is not treated otherwise, or by tightly binding with thread, or by medicines placed on it which can coagulate blood; and let it be tied and constricted accordingly.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	Whoever administers constriction tightly with fabrics or placing hot things on it, or similar things, does not benefit from it unless otherwise.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne; et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez; et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	And if this happens to anyone and they do not have medicine present, they should place their finger on the wound as we have said, and stretch it tightly until it is constricted above the wound and the vein; and it should not move but it should be moistened with cold water often so that it becomes very cold, frozen, swollen and constricted; and make inquiries in advance about those who need cauteries and medicines.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	Here begins the second book of surgical treatments
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres; et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.	We have told you in the first chapter about all diseases where fire cautery or burning medicine is required, and we have discussed their causes, instruments, forms of cauteries; and I placed that chapter from head to foot, and I will proceed with this chapter by the same way because it is easier to understand what follows.
Et ainsois que je encomence ceu, il covient, chier fil, que vos aprenez que en cest chapistre a plus de peril et de paor que ou premier des cauteres, et por ceu il covient plus grant cautele.	Furthermore, as I begin this, it is necessary for you, dear child, to learn that in this chapter there is more danger and fear than in the first of the cauteries, and because of this greater caution is required.
Car en l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’incision sus aposteme, et as cures des plaies, et a l’estraction des saiettes, et a l’incision sus la piere, et les semblans choses; ou il a doutance et paor, et en vient li mors a plusors.	For in the work of this chapter, there is often the evacuation of blood when opening a vein, and incising an abscess, and in the treatment of wounds, and in the extraction of arrows, and in cutting into stones, and similar things; where there is doubt and fear, and many die.
Et je vos amoneste que vos n’entreprenez folie.	 And I warn you not to undertake foolishness.
Car mout de manieres de gens vienent en cures.	 For many ways of people come in treatments.
si vienent de telz qui s’aïrent si avec lor maladie qu’il muerent legierement por la forsenerie qu’il trueve de sa maladie, et de la grandour de son malice; et de ces doit on avoir paor.	 Those who are so self-confident with their disease that they die easily due to the foolishness that comes from their illness and its great severity should be feared.
Et de ces i a qui te done son sens, et dit: «atendez, je sui garis»; et li maladie est despitouse.	 And among these there are those who will offer you advice, saying "wait, I am cured," but the illness is insidious.
Il ne covient mie que vos vos consentez a ces qui vienent a vos qui ont ceste maniere, mais mettez plus grant cusanson en vostre honor qu’en vostre covoitise, et n’ovrez mie folement mais saigement de ceu dont vos estes certain, et dont vos poez avoir pris et los; et usez de pronostication et de indication en cures de vos malaides a coi salus soit convertie; et ceu vos aidera a aquester bone renommee, et gloire, et memoire de loenge.	 You should not consent to those who come to you with this manner, but put more trust in your honor than in your desire, and do not act rashly but wisely from that which you are certain of, and from that which you have learned; and use diagnosis and indication in treatments of your patients so that health may be achieved; and this will help you to acquire good reputation, glory, and memory of praise.
Tres chier fil, Nostres Sires vos doint boin entendement et droiture, et se vos vuelle espireir de la sainte inspiration de sa main, amen.	Dear child, our Lord grants you good understanding and righteousness; if you wish to inspire from the holy inspiration of His hand, come.
Or je vos ai ordeneit cest chapistre en devisant par chapistres, selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre des cauteres, que je vos ai deviseit des le chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que vos trovez plus legierement ceu dont vos avrez mestier.	I have divided this chapter for your convenience, speaking one topic at a time, as the cauteries were previously described from head to feet because you will find it easier to understand what you need in this manner.
dou chief plein d’aigue	The head full of water.
Saiches que ceste maladie vient mout de fois as enfans a l’enfanter, et quant li baille estraint trop fort le chief de l’enfant; et aucune fois vient ceu de cause reponue que on ne seit.	Know that this illness often comes in children during childbirth and when the head of the child is forced too hard; sometimes it occurs for reasons unknown.
Et je ne vis onques ceste maladie fuers qu’en enfans, et a toz ces que j’ai veus se hastait li mors; et por ceu me semble qu’il me vaut mues lassier l’ovraige en teilz cures.	And I have never seen this disease in adults, except for children; and all those that I have seen hastened towards death; and because of this, it seems to me that it would be worth lessening the work in some treatments.
Et je vis .i. enfant de coi li chiés estoit plains d’aigue, et li chief engroissoit chescun jor tant qu’il ne lou pooit sostenir; et crut tant li moistor qu’il fut mors, et ceste moistor si est assemblee desoz l’os sus lou syphac, entre lou keur et l’os; et li ovraiges si est telz se li moistor est entre lou keur et l’os, et li apostemes est petis, que tu fendes emmi lou chief une fendure large; et soit ausi longe com .ij. nous, tant que li mostor corre; et vez ci la forme dou spatumile:	And I have seen one child whose head was full of water, and the head grew larger every day until it could no longer support it; and the moisture gathered under the skull bone between the brain and the skull; and if this moisture is under the skull and the abscesses are small, you should make a large incision in the head; and it should be as long as two fingers, so that the moisture can flow out; and here is the shape of the spatula:
Se li moistor est plus creue, et li aposteme soit plus grans, si fai .ij. fendures en maniere d’une croix, selonc ceste forme:	If the moisture is more swollen and the abscess is larger, make two incisions in the shape of a cross, according to this form:
Et se li moistor est desoz l’os, et li signes que tu vois les commissures dou chief overtes de chescune partie, et li aigue saut fuer quant tu la presses de ta main au dedens, et ceu ne t’est mie reponut: si covient que tu fendes enmi lou chief .iij. fendures selonc ceste maniere:	And if the moisture is beneath the bone, and the signs that you see the joints at the head of each part open up when you press it from within with your hand, and this does not respond: then you must make four incisions in the middle of the head according to this manner:
Et aprés l’incision estrai la moistor toute fuers.	 And after incision, remove all moisture from it.
Aprés estraint les fendures de drapelz et de poudres, et i met vin et oile, et laisse ensi jusc’a cinquieme jor; puis le deslie, et cure la plaie par tentes et par oignemens, et laisse estraindre le chief egaument, et done mengier au malaide viande seche de poc de moistor tant que li membre soit confortez et sanez.	 And after the incision, draw out linens and powders, and put vinegar and oil on it, leave it so until the fifth day; then undo it, and treat the wound with bandages and ointments, keep the swelling reduced, and let the patient eat dry meat of parched moisture as long as the limb is comfortable and healed.
Et une autre maniere d’incision est que tu regardes ou apert li grandor de l’aposteme, et li assemblé de l’aigue; car aucune fois est elle devant; aucune fois derrier; aucune fois en destre; et aucune fois en senestre.	And another way of incision is that you look where the abscess is larger, and gather the pus; for sometimes it is in front, sometimes behind, sometimes to the right, and sometimes to the left.
Taille donques lai ou li aposteme apert, et l’emplissement de l’aigue, et lou fent selonc ce que tu en as le pooir; et warde que tu ne coper l’artere; et veigne flun de sanc, si que li malaides muere dou decorrement de sanc et de l’evacuation de moistor.	Cut there where the abscess is open, and drain the pus; do as you can, and watch that you do not cut an artery; and let a vein bleed, so that the patient dies a natural death and from the evacuation of moisture.
de reume	of scrofula (a chronic disease affecting the lymph nodes, often in the neck)
Quant il avient a aucun une maladie qui est apelee «catarre» as eulz ou au pis, et li maladie est anciainne, et li cure de medicine ne profite mie, adonques li derraine cure si est li cauteres avec ceu c’on li copera les .ij. arteres.	When a disease called "cataract" occurs in the eyes or at its worst, and the disease is old, and the medicine's cure does not help at all, then the last cure is the cautery with which they will cut the two arteries.
Il covient donques, cant tu les vues coper, que li malaides faice rere son chief; aprés li frotte lou leu d’un drapel aspre tant que les arteres aperent, puis estraingne li malaides son col a tout I drapel; puis regarde ou li voine bait, et li leus de l’une et de l’autre sont aprés les oreilles, et poc sont reponues; puis signe les leus d’enche, puis cope l’une et l’autre d’un spatumile agut de II pars, tant que li taille veigne jusc’a l’os, et ceu soit par lou large dou chief.	 Therefore, when you wish to cover it, let the patient bend back his head; afterwards rub the area with a dry cloth harshly until the arteries appear, then grasp the patient's neck with the entire cloth; then look where the veins are biting, and the ears of both sides are behind them, and they are brought together; then mark the places to be cut, then take a sharp spatula of two parts, and cut each one until the incision reaches the bone, and this should be wide at the base.
Et se tu vues, boute le spatumile desoz l’artere et la cope au desus, en taillant ausi com .ij. dois au traver.	And if you see it (the artery), push the spatula under the artery and cut it above, cutting through as two fingers apart.
Et quant li voinne est copee, si saut li sans en haut continuelment fuers.	And when the vein is cut, it jumps up continuously without stopping.
Et se li artere n’apert au sentir, si covient que tu mesures la quantiteit de l’espaice de III dois, puis seigne d’enche et fent jusc’a l’os; et ceu qu’il covient dou sanc mettre fuers si est VI c/, et par aventure un poc plus ou moins, selonc ce que li malaides puet soffrir, et la repletion de l’artere; puis regarde la plaie: s’il remaint sus l’os point dou syphac, si le cope que apostemes chaus n’i veigne, puis estrain la plaie et lie, et la cure d’oignement tant qu’ele soit sanee.	 And if the artery does not open by itself, it is necessary that you measure the space of three fingers, then carefully make an incision up to the bone; and the amount of blood that needs to be removed is approximately 6 cubic centimeters, and possibly a little more or less, according to what the patient can endure, and the filling of the artery; then examine the wound: if it remains above the bone pointlessly, if the cauterized abscess does not come, then hold the wound closed and tied, and treat the wound with ointment until it is healed.
de emigrainne	of migration
Quant emigrainne anciaine vient, et catarre agut, por les moistors des larmes et les chalors en temples et sode anciene forsenee et semblans choses, et il est medicinez par manieres de cures de medicine et tout ceu ne li profite mie, si estraions les arteres des temples et lou cauterizons, si com nos avons conteit.	When the old migraine comes and the acute catarrh, because of moisture from tears and heat in temples and aged senility, accompanied by similar things, and it is treated with methods of medicine, but none of it helps him; then we must open the arteries of the temples and cauterize them as we have said.
Et li maniere de l’estraction d’elles si est que li malaides faice rere les poilz de ses temples, et entende a l’artere qui apert en la temple, car elle apert bien par son batement, et est poc reponue fuers que en aucuns homes qui sont trop froit; et s’elle est reponue, si estraigne son col li malaides d’aucuns drapelz, puis frote le leu d’aucun aspre drap, et arose le leu d’aigue chaude tant que li artere apere manifestement; puis pren le spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	And the method of extracting them is that the patient bares his temples hair, and listens to the artery that opens in the temple, as it opens well by its beating, and can be easily located except for some very cold men; and if it is located, the patient holds his neck with some cloths, then rubs the place with a harsh cloth, and anoints the place with warm water until the artery appears manifestly; then takes the spatula that has this form:
puis escorche le cuir legierement tant que tu veignes a l’artere, puis la trai en haut as pinceures, et la depart bien des toiles que sont desoz li de chescune partie; et se li artere est subtilz, si la torne a la pointe de l’uncine, puis la cope de celle partie selonc la quantiteit des II chiés.	 Then, lightly scrape the skin until you reach the artery, then pull it up to the pulleys, and carefully remove all the tissue that is underneath from each side; and if the artery is thin, turn it to the point of the scissors, then cut off that part according to the size of two fingers.
Car s’elle n’est copee, si ne saut mie li sans dou tout en tout.	 If it is not cut, it will not heal completely in all places.
Et trai dou sanc des .vj. c/, jusc’a .iij.; et se li artere est grans, si covient que tu la lies en .ij. leus d’un fil double fort de soie, que porriture n’i veigne devant le soudement de la plaie, et veigne decorremens de sanc; puis cope la superfluiteit qui est entre les .ij. liiens en celle houre meisme, et puis, se tu vues, si lou cauterize dou cautere cutellaire jusc’a l’os tant que li chiés soient copez; et c’est li muedre oevre, se li malaides n’a fievre et il est de chaude complexion.	And draw out the blood from the 7th vein, up to the 4th; and if the artery is large, it must be tied with a double thick silk thread so that pus does not come before the suturing of the wound, and bleeding comes; then cut away the excess that is between the two ligaments in the same hour, and if you see, cauterize the wound with the cautery tool up to the bone until the hairs are cut off; this is the moving operation, if the patient does not have fever and he is of a warm complexion.
Car li cauteres est aide por finir les moistors: por ceu est il de plus grant aide as moistors.	For cauteries are aid to finish moisters (a term for boils or abscesses): therefore it is a greater help to those with moisters.
Ou il covient por l’estraction des arteres que om emplisse lou leu de viel coton et mette on sus tentes bien faites; et quant on les desliera, si soit curez de medicines seches que font naistre char, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez; et se sans cort de l’artere tant dis com tu i oevres, si te haste dou coper par cautere, ou tu emple lou leu de vitriole et l’estrain a ta main que li sans soit estainchiez; et se tu n’as ceu present, si met sor le leu ton doit tant que li sans soit congelez, et arose le leu d’aigue froide tant que li sans cesse, et soit estraint si com il covient; et ceu qui est muedre et plus legier en l’estraction de l’artere est que tu cauterizes la voinne de cest cautere trenchant de .ij. pars, mais li trenchant soient bien espés por warder plus longement lor chalor.	Therefore, for the extraction of arteries it is necessary that one fill the place with old cotton and put on a well-made dressing; and when you pull them out, cure them with dry medicines that cause pus to form, and bandages, until they are healed; and if the artery breaks as much as you work, hurry to cover it with cauterization, or use vitriol and strain your hand so that the blood is coagulated; and if you don't have this available, put your finger on the place for a while until it becomes numb, then rub the place with cold water and keep straining as necessary; and those that are moving (referring to the broken arteries) and easier to extract should be cauterized with this sharp cautery of 2 parts, but they should be thick enough to hold their heat for a longer time.
Car quant li estrumens est trop tenves, si tient moins sa chalor.	For when the straw is too thin, it holds less heat.
Et doit avoir entre les .ij. coutelz .i. doit de gros d’espaice, et puis quant tu as signiet d’enche les .ij. leus, et tu mes lou fer ardant sus tant qu’il viegne jusc’a l’os, et cope la voinne en .ij. leus; et soient esloigniet entre les .ij. chiés car il n’est mie soudez de cest cautere dou tout en tout; et c’est li forme dou cautere:	And it should have between the two knives one thickness of a finger, and when you have pressed down on them for three inches, and you heat the iron hot enough so that it reaches the bone, and strike the vein in three inches; and they should be separated by two fingers because it is not always welded to this cautery altogether; and this is the form of the cautery:
des larmes	tears
Quant les larmes des eulz sont dessendans des voinnes que sont sus lou test dou chief de fuer, et il ne profite mie cure de medicine c’on i faice, et tu vois la faice dou malaide enrougir, et sent ou front ambulation si com de fremis; et sui oil sont tenve et moiste si que li poil des papieres sont cheut, et sont eschaufees les papieres, et escorchies de l’ardor des larmes, si ait mestier de ceste cure.	When the eyes are flowing down from veins that are above the testicle of the head and no medicine cure helps it, and you see the patient wrinkle his face, and his forehead trembles like with chills; and if they are tender and moist so that the hair of the scrotum falls out, and the scrotum is inflamed, and burned by the flow of tears, this requires this treatment.
Et l’apelerent li ancien «cure contuse», et est que tu faices a rere au malaide qui a ceste maladie les poilz qu’il ait ou front, puis li fai III fendures ou front igalment selonc la longesce dou front; et soit l’une des fendures ausi com II doi tout emmi lou front en avalant aval jusc’a neif, et les autres II as II costelz par desus les papieres, et te garde de l’incision des arteres que sont as II costez par desus les papieres; et aloigne ta main de la continuation des II mandibules, et soit chescune plaie la quantiteit de III dois au traver joins; et aies apparillie une piece d’esponge et mout de drapelz ses por essuer lou sanc, puis boute le spatumile agut de II pars de coi ci est li forme:	 And it was called by the ancients "contused cure", and you must do this to the patient who has this disease on his forehead; then make three cuts equally along the length of his forehead; and one of the cuts should be like if you were to move the forehead downwards, from top to bottom until the eyebrows, and the other two should be on the cheeks above the eyebrows, and be careful not to cut the arteries that are above the eyebrows; and keep your hand away from the continuation of the jaws, and each wound should be the size of three fingers joined together; and prepare a piece of sponge and a lot of cloth for wiping the blood, then insert the sharp lancet two parts of its length as shown here:
des l’incision qui est dever la temple jusc’a la seconde incision; et escorche tout le keur qui est entre les .ij. fendures a tot lou syfac qui est sus l’os, puis fai autreteil des la moiene incision jusc’a l’autre seconde, et puis estrai fuer cest spatumile.
